%%%%%%%%%%%%%bayes方法检查出第1个特征值的tezhengbilv%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

bayes_testdata(1)
bayes_testdata_train_data1_bilv =[];

result_train_data1_1lie_hanglie = size(result_train_data1_1lie);
result_train_data1_1lie_hangshu=result_train_data1_1lie_hanglie(1,1)  %tezhengfuhe的行数
result_train_data1_1lie_lieshu=result_train_data1_1lie_hanglie(1,2)       %tezhengfuhe的列数


for  j = 1:result_train_data1_1lie_hangshu
   if  bayes_testdata(1)  ~= result_train_data1_1lie(j,1)
        bayes_testdata_train_data1_bilv(1) =1;
   end
   if  bayes_testdata(1)  == result_train_data1_1lie(j,1)
        bayes_testdata_train_data1_bilv(1) = 1000*result_train_data1_1lie(j,3);
        break;
   end
end

bayes_testdata_train_data1_bilv(1)

result_train_data4_2lie_hangshu=result_train_data4_2lie_hanglie(1,1)  %tezhengfuhe的行数
result_train_data4_2lie_lieshu=result_train_data4_2lie_hanglie(1,2)       %tezhengfuhe的列数


for  j = 1:result_train_data4_2lie_hangshu
    if  bayes_testdata(2)  ~= result_train_data4_2lie(j,1)
        bayes_testdata_train_data4_bilv(2) =1;
   end
   if  bayes_testdata(2)  == result_train_data4_2lie(j,1)
        bayes_testdata_train_data4_bilv(2) = 1000*result_train_data4_2lie(j,3);
        break;
   end
end

bayes_testdata_train_data4_bilv(2)

        bayes_testdata_train_data5_bilv(29) =1;
   end
   if  bayes_testdata(29)  == result_train_data5_29lie(j,1)
        bayes_testdata_train_data5_bilv(29) = 1000*result_train_data5_29lie(j,3);
        break;
   end
end
